## D-5.12f Live SELL_ALL Design Spec — D-5.12f-LIVE-SELLALL-DESIGN-SPEC — Closed at `5165b555a3de215d18f50c758393fd6ae8479019`

D-5.12f-LIVE-SELLALL-DESIGN-SPEC is a DOCS-ONLY operator-directed phase persisting the Codex-PASS-verified D-5.12f live SELL_ALL DB-first persistence design as a permanent on-disk SAFE-class design record at `orchestrator/handoffs/D-5-12F-LIVE-SELLALL-DESIGN.md` (445 lines). The codification reproduces the round-2 design with the M2 Codex required edit applied (call-site fallback no longer mutates `attempted_payload` by appending `attempted_payload_hash`; `attempted_payload` remains the pure 9-field redacted object byte-stable with helper-internal redaction at `dashboard.js:813-823`; `attempted_payload_hash` carried only as separate top-level variable / emergency-audit-row field). The design defaults are DB-driven SELL_ALL quantity via `loadOpenPosition("live")`, pre-Kraken DB gate required (null → throw `"No open live position to sell"` BEFORE Kraken), wallet deficit (wallet < db − 1e-8) → hard throw pre-Kraken, wallet excess (wallet > db + 1e-8) → structured `log.warn` and proceed selling DB-tracked quantity only, `fetchKrakenBalance()` retained pre-Kraken solely for drift check (`bal?.error` → hard throw), `shadowRecordManualLiveClose` reused as-is, `exitEntry.exitReason = "MANUAL_SELLALL"`, `failureContext.source = "manual_live_sellall"`, `balanceCache = null` on every post-Kraken outcome (Codex v2 option (b)), `position.json` written ONLY after DB success, no JSON fallback on DB failure, no auto-retry, no Kraken cancellation, pointer-only operator-visible thrown errors, `MANUAL_LIVE_ARMED` Layer 1 / Layer 2 gates unchanged, typed-CONFIRM UI gate unchanged, Migration 008 treated as APPLIED at HEAD `189eb1be6ef6304d914671bdaedec44d389cf877`. The future code-phase touch perimeter is `dashboard.js` SELL_ALL block ONLY (estimated ~140-155 ins / ~10 del); no helper / migration / DB / `bot.js` / `scripts/` / `package*` / `position.json` / orchestrator/* changes (other than separate DOCS-ONLY closeout). ## DASH-3-POSITION-DISPLAY-CANONICALIZATION-DESIGN — Closed (Design-only PASS, no commit by the design phase itself)

DASH-3-POSITION-DISPLAY-CANONICALIZATION-DESIGN is a DESIGN-ONLY (Mode 2 per `orchestrator/PHASE-MODES.md`) operator-directed phase that produced the conversation-only design proposal for the dashboard's position-display canonicalization track addressing DASH-1 audit gaps G3.1 (`position.json` startup read; surface drift visibly when DB ↔ JSON disagree), G3.2 (all 5 dashboard data routes use the same Postgres-first position read), G3.3 (two `renderPosition` definitions need unified data shape contract), G3.4 (mode-mismatch detection across 9 HTML generators). The design proposes a sub-phase split: DASH-3.A (this design + the codification at DASH-3-POSITION-DISPLAY-CANONICALIZATION-DESIGN-SPEC), DASH-3.B (deferred — server-side payload contract normalization at `dashboard.js:1272-1275`; consolidates `getApiData`'s direct `position.json` JSON-fallback to delegate to `modeScopedSummary`), and DASH-3.C (deferred — server-side drift detection in `modeScopedSummary` at `:1378-1417` + v2 `renderPosition` drift badge at `:10797-10815`; legacy `renderPosition` at `:5453` inside `const HTML` template `:3169-7741` NOT touched due to template-escape risk). The phase produced no working-tree edit and no commit; the design output is conversation-only.

## DASH-4-PAPER-CONTROLS-CLEANUP-DESIGN — Closed (Design-only PASS, no commit by the design phase itself)

DASH-4-PAPER-CONTROLS-CLEANUP-DESIGN is a DESIGN-ONLY (Mode 2 per `orchestrator/PHASE-MODES.md`) operator-directed phase that produced the conversation-only design proposal for the dashboard's paper-mode manual-control envelope cleanup track. The design verifies all 5 paper handlers DB-first (BUY at `dashboard.js:1867-1900`, CLOSE_POSITION at `:2050-2074`, SELL_ALL at `:2227-2251`, SET_STOP_LOSS at `:2265-2280`, SET_TAKE_PROFIT at `:2290-2306`) via `loadOpenPosition("paper")` + `shadowRecordManualPaperBuy/Close/SLUpdate/TPUpdate` helpers; identifies envelope inconsistency I1 (paper CLOSE_POSITION lacks `quantity` while paper SELL_ALL includes it; both close paper positions) as the single concrete envelope drift, with I2/I3/I4 classified as defensible asymmetries / lower priority; proposes a sub-phase split DASH-4.A (1-line additive change at `:2074` adding `quantity` to paper CLOSE_POSITION return for envelope symmetry with paper SELL_ALL at `:2251`; LOW risk; addresses I1) as the narrowest safe sub-phase, with DASH-4.B (SL/TP structured price fields; addresses I3) and DASH-4.C (structured errorCode envelope; addresses I4) deferred indefinitely. The phase produced no working-tree edit and no commit; the design output is conversation-only.

## DASH-5.D-LIVE-MANUAL-CONTROL-FAILURE-TAXONOMY-CODIFICATION — Closed at `f2913dfe218944232b8a85f79d497512e2a40391`

DASH-5.D-LIVE-MANUAL-CONTROL-FAILURE-TAXONOMY-CODIFICATION is a DOCS-ONLY (Mode 3 per `orchestrator/PHASE-MODES.md`) operator-directed phase codifying the 7-class failure taxonomy from `DASH-5-LIVE-CONTROLS-DESIGN.md` §6 as a permanent on-disk SAFE-class reference at `orchestrator/handoffs/LIVE-MANUAL-CONTROL-FAILURE-TAXONOMY.md`. Scope: 4 files — 1 new SAFE-class taxonomy reference + 3 status doc updates (`orchestrator/STATUS.md`, `orchestrator/CHECKLIST.md`, `orchestrator/NEXT-ACTION.md`). The new reference distinguishes 3 `kraken_post_success_*` classes (post-Kraken DB-failure; real money moved; emergency-audit ladder routing) from 4 `db_only_*` classes (pre-Kraken DB-only failure; no Kraken interaction; throw-on-DB-failure ladder collapses).
